Reserves and Academy">Huddersfield Town Academy</a>, the club's project for identifying and developing young talent.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In an interview with <i><a href="/wiki/American_Theatre_(magazine)" class="mw-redirect" title="American Theatre (magazine)">American Theatre</a></i>, he stated that "From time to time, I have fantasies of becoming a concert pianist. I've been lucky enough through the years to work very closely with the great <a href="/wiki/Emanuel_Ax" title="Emanuel Ax">Emanuel Ax</a>. I've said to him that if I could switch places with anyone it would be with him."<sup id="cite_ref-Twenty_Questions_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Twenty_Questions-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2015, Stewart came under controversy on social media when he defended the Belfast-based Christian bakers that were penalized for discrimination after refusing to bake a cake with words reading, "Support Gay Marriage". Stewart, on his <a href="/wiki/Facebook" title="Facebook">Facebook</a> profile, defended his decision to side with the bakers saying that while he was still opposed to organized religion, "It was not because it was a gay couple that they objected, it was not because they were celebrating some sort of marriage or an agreement between them. It was the actual words on the cake they objected to. Because they found the words offensive. I would support their rights to say no, this is personally offensive to my beliefs, I will not do it." The Christian Bakers would ultimately win in a narrow landmark Supreme Court decision for the United Kingdom, almost simultaneously as a <a href="/wiki/Masterpiece_Cakeshop_v._Colorado_Civil_Rights_Commission" title="Masterpiece Cakeshop v. Colorado Civil Rights Commission">similar case in the United States</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Stewart is also an avid car enthusiast; he is regularly seen at <a href="/wiki/Silverstone_Circuit" title="Silverstone Circuit">Silverstone</a> during <a href="/wiki/British_Grand_Prix" title="British Grand Prix">British Grand Prix</a> weekends. He conducted the podium interview with the top 3 finishers in the <a href="/wiki/2017_Canadian_Grand_Prix" title="2017 Canadian Grand Prix">2017 Canadian Grand Prix</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> On a 2003 appearance on <i><a href="/wiki/Top_Gear_(2002_TV_series)" title="Top Gear (2002 TV series)">Top Gear</a></i> he set a lap time of 1 min 50 secs on the "Star in a Reasonably Priced Car" feature. He holds an <a href="/wiki/Motor_Sports_Association" title="Motor Sports Association">MSA</a> competition licence and competed in the 2012 <a href="/wiki/Silverstone_Classic" title="Silverstone Classic">Silverstone Classic</a> Celebrity Challenge race, finishing ninth, 3m 02.808 secs behind winner <a href="/wiki/Kelvin_Fletcher" title="Kelvin Fletcher">Kelvin Fletcher</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> During 2012, Stewart met his racing hero <a href="/wiki/Stirling_Moss" title="Stirling Moss">Stirling Moss</a> for the <a href="/wiki/BBC_Two" title="BBC Two">BBC Two</a> documentary <i>Racing Legends</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In regard to religion, Stewart, as well as his wife, is an <a href="/wiki/Atheist" class="mw-redirect" title="Atheist">atheist</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Honours">Honours</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Patrick_Stewart&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Honours">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Having lived in Los Angeles for many years, Stewart moved back to England in 2004, in part to return to work in the theatre.<sup id="cite_ref-back_on_stage_10-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-back_on_stage-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> In the same year, Stewart was appointed <a href="/wiki/Chancellor_(education)" title="Chancellor (education)">chancellor</a><sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> of the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Huddersfield" title="University of Huddersfield">University of Huddersfield</a> and subsequently as a professor of performing arts in July 2008. In these roles, Stewart has regularly attended graduation ceremonies in the UK and Hong Kong and teaches master classes for drama students.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> He stepped down from the chancellorship in July 2015, and was named chancellor emeritus in the installation ceremony for his successor, <a href="/wiki/Prince_Andrew,_Duke_of_York" title="Prince Andrew, Duke of York">Prince Andrew, Duke of York</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup> In August 2016 a building at the university was renamed the "Sir Patrick Stewart Building".<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Stewart was appointed an <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_British_Empire" title="Order of the British Empire">Officer of the Order of the British Empire</a> (OBE) in the <a href="/wiki/2001_New_Year_Honours" title="2001 New Year Honours">2001 New Year Honours</a> for services to acting and the cinema and a <a href="/wiki/Knight_Bachelor" title="Knight Bachelor">Knight Bachelor</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2010_New_Year_Honours" title="2010 New Year Honours">2010 New Year Honours</a> for services to drama.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> Stewart's knighthood was conferred by Queen <a href="/wiki/Elizabeth_II" title="Elizabeth II">Elizabeth II</a> at an <a href="/wiki/Investiture" title="Investiture">investiture</a> ceremony at <a href="/wiki/Buckingham_Palace" title="Buckingham Palace">Buckingham Palace</a> on 2 June 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In July 2011, Stewart received an Honorary <a href="/wiki/Doctorate_of_Letters" class="mw-redirect" title="Doctorate of Letters">Doctorate of Letters</a> (D.Litt.) from the <a href="/wiki/University_of_East_Anglia" title="University of East Anglia">University of East Anglia</a><sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> and in July 2014 a D.Litt. from the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Leeds" title="University of Leeds">University of Leeds</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> In May 2015, Stewart received an Honorary Doctorate (Dr.h.c.) from the <a href="/wiki/Vrije_Universiteit_Brussel" title="Vrije Universiteit Brussel">Vrije Universiteit Brussel</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> He is an Emeritus Fellow of <a href="/wiki/St_Catherine%27s_College,_Oxford" title="St Catherine&#39;s College, Oxford">St Catherine's College, Oxford</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Stewart carried the Olympic torch in July 2012 as part of the official relay for the <a href="/wiki/2012_London_Summer_Olympics" class="mw-redirect" title="2012 London Summer Olympics">2012 London Summer Olympics</a> and stated it was an experience he "will never forget", adding that it was better than any movie première.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In a 2018 poll for <a href="/wiki/Yorkshire_Day" title="Yorkshire Day">Yorkshire Day</a>, Stewart was ranked the third greatest Yorkshireman ever behind <a href="/wiki/Monty_Python" title="Monty Python">Monty Python</a> comedian <a href="/wiki/Michael_Palin" title="Michael Palin">Michael Palin</a>, and fellow actor <a href="/wiki/Sean_Bean" title="Sean Bean">Sean Bean</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Stewart currently shares the <a href="/wiki/Guinness_World_Record" class="mw-redirect" title="Guinness World Record">Guinness World Record</a> for longest career as a live-action <a href="/wiki/Marvel_superhero" class="mw-redirect" title="Marvel superhero">Marvel superhero</a> for his portrayal of <a href="/wiki/Professor_X" title="Professor X">Professor X</a> with <a href="/wiki/Hugh_Jackman" title="Hugh Jackman">Hugh Jackman</a>, who holds his for his portrayal of <a href="/wiki/Wolverine_(character)" title="Wolverine (character)">Wolverine</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Theatrical_performances">Theatrical performances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Patrick_Stewart&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Theatrical performances">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Patrick_Stewart_signing_autographs.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Patrick_Stewart_signing_autographs.jpg/220px-Patrick_Stewart_signing_autographs.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="212" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Patrick_Stewart_signing_autographs.jpg/330px-Patrick_Stewart_signing_autographs.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Patrick_Stewart_signing_autographs.jpg/440px-Patrick_Stewart_signing_autographs.jpg 2x" data-file-width="500" data-file-height="482" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Patrick_Stewart_signing_autographs.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Patrick Stewart signing autographs following a production of <i>Hamlet</i> at the RSC in July 2008</div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Royal_Shakespeare_Company">Royal Shakespeare Company</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Patrick_Stewart&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Royal Shakespeare Company">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Stewart has been a prolific actor in performances by the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Shakespeare_Company" title="Royal Shakespeare Company">Royal Shakespeare Company</a>, appearing in more than 60 productions.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup> His first appearance was in 1966 in <i><a href="/wiki/The_Investigation" title="The Investigation">The Investigation</a></i> and in the years that followed he became a core member of the company, taking on three or four major roles each season.<sup id="cite_ref-Trowbridge_125-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Trowbridge-125">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Performances">Performances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Patrick_Stewart&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Performances">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Filmography">Filmography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Patrick_Stewart&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Filmography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Film">Film</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Patrick_Stewart&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Film">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="wikitable sortable">

<tbody><tr>
<th>Year
</th>
<th>Title
</th>
<th width="100">Role
</th>
<th class="unsortable">Notes
</th></tr>
<tr>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Patrick_Stewart&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: decimal;">
<div class="mw-references-wrap"><ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-79"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-79">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Patrick Stewart's regular <i>Star Trek</i> character <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard" title="Jean-Luc Picard">Captain Picard</a> had no children in the series (barring an impostor in the episode "<a href="/wiki/Bloodlines_(Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation)" title="Bloodlines (Star Trek: The Next Generation)">Bloodlines</a>"). In the episode "<a href="/wiki/The_Inner_Light_(Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation)" title="The Inner Light (Star Trek: The Next Generation)">The Inner Light</a>", Daniel Stewart played Batai, son of Kamin, an alternate persona which Picard had unknowingly taken on for the purposes of that single episode's plot.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-80"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-80">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">In William Shatner's 2011 film <i><a href="/wiki/The_Captains_(film)" title="The Captains (film)">The Captains</a></i>, Stewart stated: "I have two major regrets, and they're both to do with the failure of – my failure in – my marriages."</span>
</li>
</ol></div></div>
